	?x4 a efo:EFO_0000399 .

### ANSWER:

	?x2 <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?x2_common .
	?x0 <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?x0_common .
	?x0 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?x0_label.
}

### SPARQL:iconductor?description?x0&anatomicalentity?x1&postjuvenilestage?x2&apoc1?x3

### ANSWER:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>

PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>

	?x0 a orth:Gene .
	?x0 genex:isExpressedIn ?x1.
	?x0 rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?x1 a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?x1 genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?x2 .
	?x2 a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?x2 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?x1 genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?x3 .
	?x3 a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?x3 rdfs:label "human" .
	?x0 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?x0_description.
}

### EXPLANATION:

    WHERE { 
        ?x0 a orth:Gene .
        ?x0 genex:isExpressedIn ?x1.
        ?x0 rdfs:label "APOC1" .
        ?x1 a genex:ExpressionCondition.
        ?x1 genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?x2 .
        ?x2 a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
        ?x2 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
        ?x1 genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?x3 .
        ?x3 a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
        ?x3 rdfs:label "human" .
        ?x0 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?x0_description.
    }

### DESCRIPTION:
This query requires the orth:Gene, genex:isExpressedIn, genex:ExpressionCondition, genex:hasAnatomicalEntity, anatomicalentity and rdfs:label.

### DETAIL:

The expression condition has the anatomical entity. That anatomical entity has the label. The expression condition has the gene. That gene has the label rdfs:label. The anatomical entity has the label. The anatomical entity has the description. That description has the label <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description>.

### EXTENSION:
The anatomical entity can also have the label anatomicalentity.

### SPARQL:omitempty_expression_level_score

### ANSWER:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>

	?x1condition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?x6 .
	?x6 rdfs:label ?x6Name .
	?x1condition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?x8 .

	?x1condition genex:hasSex "any".
	?x1condition genex:hasStrain ?x9 .
	?x9 a efo:EFO_0000392.
	?x9 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?x0 orth:organism ?x10 .
	?x10 obo:RO_0002162  ?x11 .
	?x11 a up:Taxon .
	?x11 up:commonName "human" .
	?x1 <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?x1_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	FILTER(   ?x4 != obo:GO_0005575   )
	FILTER(   ?x4 != ?x6   )
}

### INSTRUCTION

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the human gene APOC1 is expressed in the post-juvenile stage? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the strain label and the developmental stage label and the developmental stage description and the gene identifier.

### SPARQL:iconductor.ebi.ac.uk/sparql?query=### INSTRUCTION:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?x1 ?x4_label ?x6 ?x7 ?x0_identifier ?x2 ?x2Name ?x4 ?x5 ?x5_label ?x4_description ?x7_scientificname ?x0 ?x7_commonname WHERE { 
	?x0 a orth:Gene .
	?x0 genex:isExpressedIn ?x1.
	?x1 a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?x0 rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?x1 genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?x2 .
	?x2 a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?x2 rdfs:label ?x2Name .
	?x1 genex:hasAnatomicalEntity obo:GO_0005575 .
	?x1 genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?x4 .
	?x4 a efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?x4 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?x1 genex:hasSex "any".
	?x1 genex:hasStrain ?x5 .
	?x5 a efo:EFO_0000110 .
	?x5 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?x0 orth:organism ?x6 .
	?x6 obo:RO_0002162  ?x7 .
	?x7 a up:Taxon .
	?x7 up:commonName "human" .

### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the human gene APOC1 is expressed in the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain, sex, and cell type? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene expression has expression level score and the gene expression has false discovery rate p-value and the gene see also and the gene identifier.

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?x1condition ?x8 ?x9 ?x0_identifier ?x7 ?x4_label ?x4_description ?x4 ?x4Name ?x1_hasexpressionlevelscore ?x1 ?x3 ?x9_scientificname ?x6 ?x0 ?x0_seealso ?x1_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value ?x9_commonname WHERE { 
	?x0 a orth:Gene .
	?x1 a genex:Expression .
	?x1 genex:hasExpressionCondition ?x1condition .
	?x1 genex:hasExpressionLevel ?x3 .
	?x1 genex:hasSequenceUnit ?x0 .
	?x0 rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?x1condition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?x1condition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?x4 .
	?x1condition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity obo:GO_0005575 .
	?x4 a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?x4 rdfs:label ?x4Name .
	?x1condition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?x6 .
	?x6 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?x1condition genex:hasSex "any".
	?x1condition genex:hasStrain ?x7 .
	?x7 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?x0 orth:organism ?x8 .
	?x8 obo:RO_0002162  ?x9 .
	?x9 a up:Taxon .
	?x9 up:commonName "human" .
	?x9 <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?x9_scientificname.
	?x9 <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?x9_commonname.
	?x4 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?x4_label.
	?x4 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?x4_description.
	?x1 <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?x1_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?x1 <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?x1_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value.
	?x0 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?x0_seealso.
	?x0 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier> ?x0_identifier.
	FILTER(                 ?x4 !=  obo:GO_0005575                 )
}

### UPDATE QUERY

### ANSWER:

### DEMO:

### EXPLANATION:

The anatomical entity description is not provided because the anatomical entity is not described.

### See also:

<link rel="stylesheet" href="https://www.ldc.upf.es/wiki/sparql">
<script src="https://www.ldc.upf.es/wiki/sparql"></script>
<script>
// Configure SPARQL endpoint URL and request metadata.
// See: https://www.ldc.upf.es/wiki/conventions#metadata
const con = {
    url: "https://www.ebi.ac.uk/europepmc/rest/api/document/12",
    request: true,
    select: "hasAnatomicalEntity",
    description: "What are the anatomical entities where the APOC1 Homo sapiens gene is expressed? Provide also the anatomical entity description."
};

// Execute SPARQL query.
const result = SPARQL(con);

// Process the result.
result.process(function(error, result) {
    if (error) {
        console.error(error);
    } else {
        const entities = result["hasAnatomicalEntity"];
        entities.forEach(function(entity) {
            console.log(entity);
        });
        const descriptions = result["hasAnatomicalEntity"]["_description"];
        descriptions.forEach(function(description) {
            console.log(description);
        });
    }
});
</script>

98:
### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the developmental stage label and the developmental stage description and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene expression has expression level score and the gene expression has false discovery rate p-value and the gene see also.

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?x6 ?x8_description ?x1 ?x3 ?x1condition ?x4_description ?x8 ?x10_scientificname ?x1_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value ?x9 ?x4_label ?x1_hasexpressionlevelscore ?x0_seealso ?x8_label ?x10 ?x4 ?x4Name ?x6Name ?x0 ?x10_commonname WHERE { 
	?x0 a orth:Gene .
	?x1 a genex:Expression .
	?x1 genex:hasExpressionCondition ?x1condition .
	?x1 genex:hasExpressionLevel ?x3 .
	?x1 genex:hasSequenceUnit ?x0 .
	?x0 rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?x1condition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?x1condition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?x4 .
	?x4 a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?x4 rdfs:label ?x4Name .
	?x1condition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?x6 .
	?x6 rdfs:label ?x6Name .
	?x1condition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?x8 .
	?x8 rdf:type efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?x8 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?x0 orth:organism ?x9 .
	?x9 obo:RO_0002162  ?x10 .
	?x10 a up:Taxon .
	?x10 up:commonName "human" .
	?x10 <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?x10_scientificname.
	?x10 <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?x10_commonname.
	?x8 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?x8_label.
	?x8 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?x8_description.
	?x4 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?x4_label.
	?x4 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?x4_description.
	?x1 <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?x1_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?x1 <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?x1_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value.
	?x0 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?x0_seealso.
	FILTER(                 ?x4 !=  obo:GO_0005575                 )
	FILTER(                 ?x4 != ?x6                 )
}

### OUTPUT:
### x4_label: Human gene expression condition anatomical entity <http://purl.org/genex#AnatomicalEntity>
### x4: <http://purl.org/genex#AnatomicalEntity>
### x4Name: Anatomical entity
### x6_label: Human gene expression condition anatomical entity <http://purl.org/genex#AnatomicalEntity>
### x6: <http://purl.org/genex#AnatomicalEntity>
### x6Name: Anatomical entity
### x8_label: Human developmental stage <EFO_0000399>
### x8: EFO_0000399
### x8_description: Human developmental stage
### x1_hasexpressionlevelscore: False

### INSTRUCTION

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the strain label and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene expression has expression level score and the gene expression has false discovery rate p-value and the gene see also and the gene description and the gene label.

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?x6 ?x1 ?x3 ?x1condition ?x4_description ?x11_scientificname ?x9_label ?x10 ?x4_label ?x1_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value ?x11 ?x4 ?x4Name ?x6Name ?x0_label ?x0_description ?x0 ?x0_seealso ?x11_commonname WHERE { 
	?x0 a orth:Gene .
	?x1 a genex:Expression .
	?x1 genex:hasExpressionCondition ?x1condition .
	?x1 genex:hasExpressionLevel ?x3 .
	?x1 genex:hasSequenceUnit ?x0 .
	?x0 rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?x1condition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?x1condition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?x4 .
	?x4 a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?x4 rdfs:label ?x4Name .
	?x1condition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?x6 .
	?x6 rdfs:label ?x6Name .
	?x1condition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?x8 .
	?x8 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?x1condition genex:hasSex "any".
	?x1condition genex:hasStrain ?x9 .
	?x9 a efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?x9 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?x0 orth:organism ?x10 .
	?x10 obo:RO_0002162  ?x11 .
	?x11 a up:Taxon .
	?x11 up:commonName "human" .
	?x11 <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?x11_scientificname.
	?x11 <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?x11_commonname.
	?x9 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?x9_label.
	?x4 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?x4_label.
	?x4 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?x4_description.
	?x1 <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?x1_hasexpressionlevel.
	?x1 <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?x1_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value.
	?x0 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?x0_seealso.
	?x0 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?x0_description.
	?x0 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?x0_label.
	FILTER(                       ?x4 != obo:GO_0005575                       )
	FILTER(                       ?x4 != ?x6                       )
}
